    <P align=justify><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>These transactions were in the normal course of operations and were measured at the exchange value which represented the amount of consideration established and agreed to by the related parties.</FONT></P>
    <P align=left><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>CRITICAL ACCOUNTING ESTIMATES</FONT></B></P>
    <P align=justify><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>The preparation of the Company&#146;s financial statements requires management to make estimates and assumptions regarding future events. These estimates and assumptions affect the reported amounts of certain assets and liabilities, and disclosure of contingent liabilities.</FONT></P>
    <P align=justify><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Significant areas requiring the use of management estimates include the determination of impairment of equipment, environmental and reclamation obligations, rates for amortization, variables used in determining stock-based compensation and assessments of control of variable interest entities. These estimates are based on management&#146;s best judgment. Factors that could affect these estimates include risks inherent in mineral exploration and development, changes in reclamation requirements, changes in government policy and changes in foreign exchange rates.</FONT></P>
    <P align=justify><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Management has assessed the carrying value of its assets and does not believe the remaining assets have suffered any impairment.</FONT></P>
    <P align=justify><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>The Company does not believe it has incurred any material environmental liabilities to date. The Company has the responsibility to perform reclamation in certain jurisdictions upon completion of drilling. The costs to complete this reclamation are immaterial and are expensed when incurred.</FONT></P>
    <P align=justify><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Management has made significant assumptions and estimates in determining the fair market value of stock-based compensation granted to employees and non-employees and the value attributed to various warrants and broker warrants issued on financings. These estimates have an effect on the stock-based compensation expense recognized and the contributed surplus and share capital balances on the Company&#146;s balance sheet. Management has made estimates of the life of stock options and warrants, the expected volatility and expected dividend yields that could</FONT> <font face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>materially affect the fair market value of these types of securities. The estimates were chosen after reviewing the historical life of the Company&#146;s options and analyzing share price history to determine volatility.</font></P>
    <P align=center><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>10</FONT></P>
    <HR style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always" align=center width="100%" noShade SIZE=1>
    <!--$$/page=-->
    <A name="page_11"></A>
    <P align=left><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>CHANGES IN ACCOUNTING POLICIES</FONT></B></P>
    <TABLE cellSpacing=0 border=0>
      <TR>
        <TD vAlign=top noWrap width="2%"><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>a)</FONT></B>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; </TD>
        <TD width="98%"><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Goodwill and Other Intangible Assets</FONT></B></TD>
      </TR>
    </TABLE>
    <P align=left><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Effective 1 December 2008, the Company adopted the Canadian Institute of Chartered Accountants (&#147;CICA&#148;) Handbook Section 3064 &#147;</FONT><I><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Goodwill and Other Intangible Assets</FONT></I><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>&#148;. The new requirements of Section 3064 are for recognition, measurement, presentation and disclosure. Section 3064 replaces Section 3062, &#147;</FONT><I><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Goodwill and Other Intangible Assets</FONT></I><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>&#148;. The new standard establishes revised standards for the recognition, measurement, presentation and disclosure of goodwill and intangible assets. The new standard also provides guidance for the treatment of preproduction and start-up costs and requi
res that these costs be expensed as incurred.</FONT></P>
    <TABLE cellSpacing=0 border=0>
      <TR>
        <TD vAlign=top noWrap width="2%"><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>b)</FONT></B>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; </TD>
        <TD width="98%"><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Accounting Guideline No. 11</FONT></B></TD>
      </TR>
    </TABLE>
    <P align=left><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>In 2001, the CICA issued Accounting Guideline No. 11, which covers the Company&#146;s exploration activities. In the past, the Company has capitalized certain exploration costs on mineral properties that were not covered by feasibility studies, whereas under the new guideline, the Company was required to expense these amounts in the year incurred. Effective 1 January 2001, the Company adopted these new recommendations on a retroactive basis. The impact as at 1 January 2001 of the adoption of these new recommendations was to reduce mineral properties by $561,257 and to increase deficit, accumulated during the exploration stage by $561,257.</FONT></P>
    <P align=left><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>NEW ACCOUNTING PRONOUNCEMENTS</FONT></B></P>
    <P align=left><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Future Changes in Accounting Policies International Financial Reporting Standards (&#147;IFRS&#148;)</FONT></B></P>
    <P align=left><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>In 2006, the Canadian Accounting Standards Board (&#147;AcSB&#148;) published a new strategic plan that will significantly affect financial reporting requirements for Canadian companies. The AcSB strategic plan outlines the convergence of Canadian GAAP with IFRS over an expected five year transitional period. In February 2008 the AcSB announced that 2011 is the changeover date for publicly-listed companies to use IFRS, replacing Canada&#146;s own GAAP. The date is for interim and annual financial statements relating to fiscal years beginning on or after January 1, 2011. The transition date of January 1, 2011, will require the restatement for comparative purposes of amounts reported by the Company for the year ended November 30, 2011. While the Company has begun assessing the adoption of IFRS for 2011, the financial reporting impact of the transition to IFRS cannot be reasonably estimated at this time.</FONT></P>
    <P align=left><B><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>FINANCIAL INSTRUMENTS AND OTHER INSTRUMENTS</FONT></B></P>
    <P align=left><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Fair value - The fair value of cash and cash equivalents, amounts receivable and accounts payable and accrued liabilities approximates their carrying value due to the short-term nature of these financial instruments.</FONT></P>
    <P align=left><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Exchange risk - The Company operates solely in Canada and therefore is subject to minimal foreign currency risk arising from changes in exchange rates with other currencies.</FONT></P>
    <P align=left><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Interest rate risk - The Company is exposed to interest rate risk on its short-term investments, but this risk relates only to investments held to fund future activities and does not affect the Company&#146;s current operating activities.</FONT></P>
    <P align=left><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>Credit risk - The Company places its temporary investment funds with government and bank debt securities and is subject to minimal credit risk with regard to temporary investments.</FONT></P>
    <P align=left><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>The Company does not have any risk associated with &#147;other instruments&#148;; that is, instruments that may be settled by the delivery of non-financial assets.</FONT></P>
    <P align=center><FONT face="TimesNewRomanPSMT,Times New Roman,Times,serif" size=2>11</FONT></P>

(the &quot;issuer&quot;) for the interim period ended February 28, 2009.</P>
<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">&nbsp;</P>

<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">3. <B><I>Fair presentation:</I></B> Based on my knowledge, having exercised reasonable diligence, the interim financial statements together with the other financial information included in the interim filings fairly present in all material respects the financial condition, results of operations and cash flows of the issuer, as of the date of and for the periods presented in the interim filings.</P>

        <TD style="border-left:1px solid #000000; border-right:1px solid #000000; border-bottom:1px solid #000000" width=1578.333 colspan=2><P style="line-height:11pt; margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:5px; font-family:Arial; font-size:9pt">The issuer's certifying officers are responsible for ensuring that processes are in place to provide them with sufficient knowledge to support the representations they are making in this certificate. Investors should be aware that inherent limitations on the ability of certifying officers of a venture issuer to design and implement on a cost effective basis DC&amp;P and ICFR as defined in NI 52-109 may result in additional risks to the quality, reliability, transparency and timeliness of interim and annual filings and other reports provided under securities legislation.</P></TD>
      </TR>
    </TABLE>
    <P style="margin:0px"><BR>
    </P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR>
    <HR noShade SIZE=1 style="page-break-after:always">
    <P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; font-family:Arial" align=center><B>FORM 52-109FV2</B></P>
    <P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; font-family:Arial" align=center><B>CERTIFICATION OF INTERIM FILINGS</B></P>
    <P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; font-family:Arial" align=center><B>VENTURE ISSUER BASIC CERTIFICATE</B></P>
    <P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; font-family:Arial" align=center>&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; font-family:Arial">I, Gordon Steblin, Chief Financial Officer of Alberta Star Development Corp., certify the following:</P>
    <P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">1. <B><I>Review:</I></B> I have reviewed the interim financial statements and interim MD&amp;A (together, the &quot;interim filings&quot;) of Alberta Star Development Corp. (the &quot;issuer&quot;) for the interim period ended February 28, 2009.</P>
<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">2. <B><I>No misrepresentations:</I></B> Based on my knowledge, having exercised reasonable diligence, the interim filings do not contain any untrue statement of a material fact or omit to state a material fact required to be stated or that is necessary to make a statement not misleading in light of the circumstances under which it was made, with respect to the period covered by the interim filings.</P>
<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:5.533px; margin-bottom:5.533px; padding-left:28.8px; font-family:Arial">3. <B><I>Fair presentation:</I></B> Based on my knowledge, having exercised reasonable diligence, the interim financial statements together with the other financial information included in the interim filings fairly present in all material respects the financial condition, results of operations and cash flows of the issuer, as of the date of and for the periods presented in the interim filings.</P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Arial">&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Arial">Date: April 27, 2009</P>
